    $(document).ready(function(){
 			if( isBreakpoint('md') || isBreakpoint('lg') ) {
 				$("[data-toggle='dropdown']").on("click", function(e){
 					if((e.which == "1") && $(this).is(":hover") && !$(this).parents(".dropdown").hasClass("open")){
 						e.stopImmediatePropagation();
 						if ($(this).attr('target') !== "_blank" ) {
 							document.location=$(this).attr("href");
 						}
 					}
 				});
 			}
 			function isBreakpoint( alias ) {
 				return $('.device-' + alias).is(':visible');
 			}
 
 			// makes href="tel:#"s valid for browsers
 			$('a[href^="tel"]').each( function(){
 				$(this).attr('href', 'tel:' + $(this).attr('href').replace(/\D+/g,""));
 			});
 
 			// makes href="fax:#"s valid for browsers
 			$('a[href^="fax"]').each( function(){
 				$(this).attr('href', 'fax:' + $(this).attr('href').replace(/\D+/g,""));
 			});
 
 			// prevents footer collapse animation on viewports when the
 			// collapse element is already forced open
       $('footer [data-toggle="collapse"]').on('click', function(e){
         if ($('footer .collapse:not(.in)').is(':visible')) {
           e.preventDefault();
           e.stopPropagation();
         } else {
           return true;
         }
       });
 
 		});
   </script>

       <div>
        <h1>
         Welcome to
         <span>
          Harley-Davidson
          <span>
           ®
          </span>
          of
         </span>
         Greenville
        </h1>
        <span>
         Greenville, South Carolina
        </span>
        <div class="welcome-text">
         <p>
          We strive to make the atmosphere at Harley-Davidson of Greenville pleasant and rewarding to customers and employees. In July 2004 Harley-Davidson of Greenville opened a new and larger location at 30 Chrome Drive with over 35,000 sq. ft. of Harley awesomeness.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Today Harley-Davidson of Greenville offers customers high quality merchandise with the utmost respect to our customers and the Harley-Davidson brand. Our number one priority is to service our customers to the best of our ability and help them live the dream of owning a Harley-Davidson. We are dedicated to making Harley-Davidson of Greenville a comfortable and trustworthy environment for Harley-Davidson enthusiasts of all ages and walks of life.
         </p>
        </div>
        <a href="/learn-about-us--info">
         <span>
          Learn More About Us
         </span>
        </a>
